void initVector(int v[], int n) {
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        v[i] = i * 2;
    }
}

void printVector(int v[], int n) {
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        printf("%d ", v[i]);
    }
    printf("\n");
}

int binsearch_kr(int x, int v[], int n) {
    int low = 0;
    int high = n - 1;
    while (low <= high) {
        int mid = (low + high) / 2;
        if (x < v[mid]) {
            high = mid - 1;
        } else if (x > v[mid]) {
            low = mid + 1;
        } else {
            return mid;
        }
    }
    return -1;
}

int binsearch(int x, int v[], int n) {
    int low = 0;
    int high = n - 1;
    int mid;
    while (low <= high) {
        mid = (low + high) / 2;
        if (x < v[mid]) {
            high = mid - 1;
        } else if (x > v[mid]) {
            low = mid + 1;
        } else {
            return mid;
        }
    }
    return -1;
}

int main() {
    int size = 10;
    int testArray[size];
    initVector(testArray, size);

    printf("Array: ");
    printVector(testArray, size);

    test_binsearch(binsearch, 6, testArray, size);

    return 0;
}

int test_binsearch(int v[], int size, int x) {
    int low = 0;
    int high = size - 1;

    while (low <= high) {
        int mid = low + (high - low) / 2;

        if (v[mid] == x) {
            return mid;
        } else if (v[mid] < x) {
            low = mid + 1;
        } else {
            high = mid - 1;
        }
    }

    return -1; // Return -1 if 'x' is not found in the array
}

```c
#include <stdio.h>

// Incomplete binsearch function
int binsearch(int x, int v[], int n)
{
    int low, high, mid;
    
    low = 0;
    high = n - 1;
    
    while (low <= high)
    {
        mid = (low + high) / 2;
        
        if (x < v[mid])
        {
            high = mid - 1;
        }
        else if (x > v[mid])
        {
            low = mid + 1;
        }
        else // x is found
        {
            return mid;
        }
    }
    
    // x not found
    return -1;
}

    if (result != -1)
    {
        printf("Element found at index: %d\n", result);

    }
}
```

```c
#include <stdio.h>

int binsearch(int x, int v[], int n)
{
  int low, high, mid;

  low = 0;
  high = n - 1;

  while (low <= high)
  {
    mid = (low + high) / 2;
    if (x < v[mid])
      high = mid - 1;
    else if (x > v[mid])
      low = mid + 1;
    else
      return mid;
  }

  return -1;
}

    printf("Value %d found at index %d\n", x, result);
  else
    printf("Value %d not found in the array\n", x);

  test_nr++;
}

{

  int x = 5;
  int n = sizeof(v) / sizeof(v[0]);

  return 0;
```
}

int binsearch(int x, int v[], int n)
{
  int low, high, mid;
  
  low = 0;
  high = n - 1;
  while (low <= high) {
    mid = (low + high) / 2;
    if (x < v[mid])
      high = mid - 1;
    else if (x > v[mid])
      low = mid + 1;
    else
      return mid; // Found match
  }
  return -1; // No match
}

First element of precision:0.0
Sequence Matcher Similarity Precision:0.011009174311926606
Cosine Similarity Precision:0.0

Parse State: 154	Cursor Position: 1140 17

                return -1;
}
